> **ÔľÂ RE-PASS ROUND 5 (2026-07-16) ÔÇö hive-codex found my round-4 fix STILL had two fail-opens. FIXED. NO PUSH.**
> - **docs allowlist filter fail-OPEN (HIGH) ÔÇö FIXED.** Round 4 fixed the primary `scan()` grep but left the
>   allowlist step as `{ grep -vixE ÔÇŽ || true; }`. That `|| true` ALSO swallowed a filter tool failure (rc>1): if
>   the allowlist grep errored while upstream emitted a REAL MAC, the leak was erased and the pipeline read clean.
>   Reproduced. Fixed with an `allow_filter` helper (same rc discipline as `scan`): rc0/1 = success, rc>1 propagates
>   = fail-CLOSED. Verified: allowlist-grep rc2 + upstream real MAC now EXITS NONZERO, not clean.
> - **end-to-end KATs discarded exit status (MED) ÔÇö FIXED.** The `hygiene_scan_tree` KATs used `[ -n "$(ÔÇŽ)" ]` /
>   `[ -z ÔÇŽ ]`, which drop the command-substitution status, so a scanner crash that emitted a finding (or emitted
>   nothing) false-passed. Replaced with an `e2e MODE NAME` helper that captures output AND status separately:
>   flag = findings+rc0, clean = empty+rc0, failclosed = rcÔëá0. The empty-tree KAT is the one explicit rcÔëá0 case.
> - RESUME durable line corrected (no longer claims blanket `|| true`); strongest temp-repo mixed-EUI/mixed-separator
>   replay recorded PASS (both mixed orders + mixed EUI-64 + underscore/-if00 path form all flag [MAC] end-to-end;

## ­čöČ XIAO BENCH decode-support (android, 2026-07-12) ÔÇö golden frames handed + board-health cleared (commit 95d5148)
android hit two things decoding the XIAO USB egress: (1) InvalidRouteLen on live captures, (2) the stream went QUIET.
**Both answered via fleet send + persisted to docs/BENCH-BOARD-FACTS.md.** (1) ROOT CAUSE = capture drop, NOT a
decoder bug: `dd bs=1` byte-drops the egress (27ÔÇô30B vs true fixed 31B); byte0=0x06 sets has_route, so ONE dropped
byte reads data[12] as rlen=0x00 = InvalidRouteLen exactly. Handed a byte-exact GOLDEN frame from canonical
`r2_wire::encode_compact` (round-trips decode_compact): compact 31B = `0653000164cedbf305fe0701011234a10018eaa101182a0102030405060708`;
R2-USB DATA record 33B = `1f00ÔÇŽ` (1f00 = payload_len 31 LE). Emitter LANDED = `crates/r2-hive-bin/examples/gen_golden_compact_frame.rs`
(regen: `cargo run -p r2-hive --example gen_golden_compact_frame`). 0xA1 sighting golden already byte-exact in
dfr1195 `USB-BEACON-SIGHTING-FORMAT.md` KAT. (2) QUIET = peer-silence (egress is PURE forwarded LoRa RX, NO
keepalive); board still enumerated at same MAC = NOT in ROM download mode; forward-task can't wedge on a DTR toggle
(USB-JTAG egress drops-when-unread, never blocks). Did NOT touch the board.
**Ôśů BEARER-OWNER DECISIONS LOCKED (composer eb0bc75 + android, 2026-07-12):** LoRa REAL + WiFi REAL + BLE dark.
**(a) fw inject-per-transport harness CANCELLED** (composer #2 ÔÇö no no-RF sim leg needed; removed from open items).
**(b) NEW hive task #66 (composer #1), GATED on supervisor GO:** stand a 2nd LoRa node at SF7 (`benchsf7`) as the
R2-PROVISION ┬ž3.2 JOIN counterparty to the XIAO (android is phone-provisioner ONLY). Deps on GO: 2nd SX1262 board
attached (RAK DISCONNECTED ÔÇö need Roy hw) + a JOIN-role build (not keyless xiaobridge). **BLE-REAL FINALIZED (composer 0b2d0bd)** ÔÇö not skip. Reflash `xiaobridge,ble` still HELD but ADDITIVE (keeps LoRa
bridge + adds ble_task); trigger = AFTER (a) WiFi leg proven AND (b) android BlueZ central built, at a convenient
break in android's live capture. **Ôťů compile-verified locally (xtensa esp toolchain): `xiaobridge,ble,benchsf7`
builds GREEN (warnings-only) = no feature-unification blocker.** **ÔÜá compile-green Ôëá coex-proven** ÔÇö BLE+WiFi+LoRa on
the one S3 radio is metal-only at reflash time; full ELF owed at the reflash window (NOT staged now ÔÇö fw may change).
**Do-not-assume:** do NOT reflash until composer/android give the break signal. boot-banner hive_id/TG/persona/build_id
owed on next reset catch.

RE-VENDOR STEP (fresh): `\cp -r` (cp is aliased to cp -i ÔÇö use \cp/rsync, [[mcu-cargo-check-from-package-dir]]) core's crates/r2-update + crates/r2-trust Ôćĺ rak4630-fw/crates/ Ôćĺ then ÔśůDILIGENCE: review the d8e09a2..01b6f14 core diff for (a) any NEW REQUIRED ImageSink trait method the FlashSink (platforms/rak4630/src/ota.rs) must impl [core said additive/no-sig-change, but VERIFY ÔÇö staged_rollback_value already impl'd], (b) any breaking DeviceContext/verify_header change the app uses Ôćĺ Cargo.lock sync Ôćĺ build-verify the APP (platforms/rak4630, from the package dir) stays green. THEN wire the bootloader gate + app receiver loop. This is the bounded low-risk FIRST step of the build block; the gate logic (fresh-vs-resume swap safety) is the safety-critical part after it.
**ÔśůÔśůÔśů 2026-07-13 ÔÇö cad8b57 HELD (hive-codex CRITICAL, correctly caught); SUPERSEDE with a redesigned local successor (GO, compile-only, no push/flash until twin-clean).** cad8b57 (bootloader gate) + ec29da4 (re-vendor) = LOCAL commits, UNPUSHED. Parked app edits = stash 6dcfccc (embassy_boot relink @0x24000 + the insufficient 201Ôćĺ204 align). **Confirmed defects (all real vs the exact release ELF):** C1 approval guard DEAD ÔÇö gate_flag@201, 201%4Ôëá0 Ôćĺ Nvmc Unaligned Ôćĺ optimizer removed the approve write Ôćĺ NO durable approval Ôćĺ power-cut brick (most reproducible fact). C2 reject ignores STATE-erase failure Ôćĺ erased bytes copied into ACTIVE. C3 divergent geometry ÔÇö boot DFU 0x91000 vs ota.rs SLOT_B_BASE 0x7e000 vs app persona 0x12000 vs bootloader anchor 0x22000 vs app linkÔëá0x24000. C4 confirmed_seq unaligned@205, read-only, no writer, shares the OTA-META erase page (wiped next stage). H1 bare GATE_APPROVED not candidate-bound (stale APPROVED + later SWAP bypasses verify), no clear/tombstone. H2 payload bounded to DFU_LEN 444K but swap copies ACTIVE 436K (436..444K images truncate); accepts ANY payload_type + discards VerifiedUpdate (DIFF/PLUGIN swapped as firmware). H3 DeviceContext identical dev/prod (prod rejects real targeted images, bypasses battery gate). H4 persona only "sealed" ÔÇö no BPROT/ACL, app owns unrestricted Nvmc Ôćĺ app compromise rewrites anchor/bootloader. **REFUTED/PROVEN:** 4K STATE OK ((2+4┬Ě109)┬Ě4=1752B<4096) ÔÇö KEEP + assert formula; alloc stub not in ELF (r2-trust alloc DCE'd) ÔÇö keep as drift-backstop + ELF-symbol test.
**CORRECTED MAP (successor):** BOOTLOADER 0x0-0x20000 | STATE 0x20000-0x21000 (4K, proven) | OTA-META 0x21000-0x22000 (candidate prefix+approval) | PERSONA 0x22000-0x24000 | ACTIVE 0x24000-0x91000 (436K/109pg) | DFU 0x91000-0xFF000 (440K/110pg = ACTIVE+1, the documented min) | JOURNAL 0xFF000-0x100000 (4K confirmed-floor, OUTSIDE the swap). **SUCCESSOR REQUIREMENTS (GO):** (1) ONE shared geometry source (app+boot+ota.rs+persona) + build-time overlap/boundary KATs. (2) ALWAYS-VERIFY, gated on embassy-boot's OWN progress counter ÔÇö NO separate approval record/digest (supervisor Occam+security refutation 2026-07-13, VERIFIED vs embassy-boot-0.7.0 source). Why the digest was dropped: (a) the payload-SHA256 (the expensive part) is paid EITHER WAY (verify checks payload_hash; skip recomputes the digest over the same bytes) ÔÇö skip saves ONLY the Ed25519 (~tens of ms) ONCE PER OTA (fresh swap), not per boot (normal State::Boot = zero crypto); (b) the digest adds ZERO security ÔÇö a flash-writing attacker forges the skip in BOTH models (writes record = SHA256(their headerÔÇľsigÔÇľpayload); bootloader recomputes over their DFU, matches, skips), identical to forging the progress counter; both rely SOLELY on H4 ACL flash-lock. Ground truth (boot_loader.rs): read_state()==Swap for BOTH fresh & in-progress (magic-only); swap() physically ROTATES DFUÔćöACTIVE pages, so mid-swap the DFU payload is scrambled/unverifiable; at current_progress()==0 NOTHING is written yet (first op touches only the DFU scratch page at progressÔćĺ1; first DFU-payload overwrite not until progressÔëą2) Ôçĺ progress==0 is a HARD pristine-DFU guarantee. Gate: State::Swap && progress==0 Ôçĺ FRESH Ôçĺ read header+sig from OTA-META + stream pristine DFU payload Ôçĺ full verify_staged_slot (Ed25519 + SHA256==payload_hash + seq>floor) Ôçĺ PASS Ôćĺ call prepare_boot (starts swap); FAIL Ôćĺ checked-reject. State::Swap && progress>0 Ôçĺ swap already begun (scrambled) Ôçĺ NEVER verify, NEVER reject/erase Ôçĺ pass straight to prepare_boot (embassy resumes). Power-cut in the verifyÔćĺprepare window leaves progress==0 Ôçĺ next boot re-verifies pristine DFU (idempotent). The durable "already-authorized" signal is embassy-boot's progress counter itself ÔÇö no record to write/bind. NOTE: this reads STATE progress words directly (magic@0, valid-marker@WRITE_SIZE, progress@2┬ĚWRITE_SIZE+, per embassy-boot 0.7/0.12) ÔÇö KAT-pin this layout + re-verify on any embassy-boot bump. (3) checked reject ÔÇö prove STATE non-SWAP (readback) before DFU erase, else fail-stop. (4) payload gate ÔÇö 0<lenÔëĄACTIVE_LEN, PT_FIRMWARE_FULL, bootable-vector sanity, USE VerifiedUpdate. (5) split dev-bench vs prod DeviceContext (prod = persona/board/device/battery, fail-closed if unavailable). (6) confirmed floor in the SEPARATE atomic JOURNAL page + pending/confirm lifecycle, NO floor=0 fallback. (7) H4 BPROT/ACL ÔÇö NOT a permitted follow-up for a prod-compilable successor (coordinator correction 2026-07-13): the PROD bootloader build MUST apply reset-time BPROT/ACL protecting BOOTLOADER (0x0-0x20000) + PERSONA (0x22000-0x24000) so a compromised app cannot rewrite the anchor/bootloader, AND partition-wrap the app's Nvmc writes to its own regions; the ONLY unprotected build is an EXPLICITLY-NAMED dev/bench feature; a prod build without protection MUST fail-closed at COMPILE time (compile_error!/const-assert), never silently ship unprotected. Implemented WITH increment 2 (bootloader). Ôśů ACCEPTANCE (exact re-pass, coordinator 2026-07-13): there must be NO production path that boots with a WRITABLE bootloader/persona ÔÇö every prod build either boots ACL-protected or does not compile; only the explicit dev/bench feature boots unprotected. (8) falsifiers: power-cut@every write/erase/swap-boundary, stale-approval/new-candidate, map-overlap, reject-fail, floor. LOCAL commit only Ôćĺ exact hive-codex re-pass. DO-NOT-FLASH + Roy tg_pk gate stand.
**Ôśů APP-SEAM FLASHSINK SUB-INCREMENT SPEC (pickup-ready; GATED behind a clean re-review of 9135db2 ÔÇö do NOT start until re-pass clean; supervisor sequencing).** Files = `rak4630-fw/platforms/rak4630/{src/ota.rs, src/main.rs, build.rs}`. Contract (core-blessed staging ruling + my OTA-META metadata-region choice + F1):
> (1) **ota.rs consume rak-geometry:** `SLOT_B_BASE`Ôćĺ`DFU_ORIGIN` (0x91000), `SLOT_SIZE`/`capacity()`Ôćĺ`ACTIVE_LEN` (0x6D000; matches the boot gate `payload_sizeÔëĄACTIVE_LEN` bound). (2) **ÔśůF1 app-half ÔÇö FULL-SLOT ERASE:** `begin()` MUST erase the WHOLE DFU slot `DFU[0..DFU_LEN]` (not just payload-rounded), so the unauthenticated tail `DFU[payload_size..ACTIVE_LEN]` is 0xFF ÔÇö ELSE the boot gate's tail-all-0xFF assert (9135db2) REJECTS a legit image. (3) **Receiver flow (#19/#35):** use `r2_update::OtaReceiver` (import the SIGNED one BY NAME ÔÇö NOT the legacy unsigned `r2_hive_core::ota::OtaReceiver`): `new(ctx, PT_FIRMWARE_FULL, FlashSink)` Ôćĺ `push(&[u8])->Result<(RxProgress, consumed), RxError>` (preserve `sdu[consumed..]` post-package bytes) Ôćĺ `finish(self)->(AppliedUpdate, S, prefix:[u8;201])`. `abort()` idempotent + safe after a FAILED/partial `begin()`. (4) **commit_swap (ORDER = the core atomicity contract):** payloadÔćĺDFU[0..] via FlashSink (verify-before-write) Ôćĺ finish Ôćĺ write `prefix[201]` (header137+sig64) Ôćĺ `OTA_META[0..201]` Ôćĺ set STATE `[0xF0;4]` SWAP_MAGIC **LAST** (plain Nvmc; embassy-boot magic word). Crash anywhere before the magic = no swap = old image boots (safe); corrupt after = boot-gate `verify_staged_slot` Err = fail-closed. (5) persona read `0x12000`Ôćĺ`PERSONA_ORIGIN` (0x22000). (6) app `build.rs` FLASH originÔćĺ`ACTIVE_ORIGIN` (0x24000) + VTOR reloc; reconcile parked stash `6dcfccc` (KEEP its embassy_boot relink@0x24000 + VTOR; DROP the obsolete 201Ôćĺ204 align ÔÇö no approval record anymore). (7) then compile app+boot TOGETHER Ôćĺ exact hive-codex re-pass. DO-NOT-FLASH + Roy tg_pk gate stand.

Gate flow in bootloader main, BEFORE prepare_boot(): read STATE magic; if !=Swap Ôćĺ prepare_boot as normal (Boot/Revert/DfuDetach, zero crypto). If ==Swap Ôćĺ read current_progress() (STATE progress words): progress==0 (PRISTINE DFU, proven ÔÇö first swap op touches only the scratch page) Ôćĺ read 137B header + 64B sig from OTA-META prefix + stream DFU payload Ôćĺ verify_staged_slot(header, sig, dfu_payload_chunks, ctx) Ôćĺ PASS Ôćĺ prepare_boot() (begins swap); FAIL Ôćĺ checked-reject (erase STATEÔćĺreadback non-SWAPÔćĺerase DFU, else fail-stop). progress>0 (swap already begun, DFU scrambled) Ôćĺ NEVER verify, NEVER reject/erase Ôćĺ prepare_boot() (embassy resumes/reverts). **Ôťů SPEC READ @0f61c81 (scratchpad/R2-PROVISION-0f61c81.md ┬ž5.3.4 lines 448-798).** Frame vocab (R2-USB ┬ž3.7 control `[0xFF]ÔÇľCBOR({0:msg_type,1:fields})`): 4 PAIR_HELLO_HOST hostÔćĺp `{}` ┬Ě 5 PAIR_COMMIT pÔćĺhost `{1:commit(32)}` ┬Ě 13 PAIR_HOST_REVEAL hostÔćĺp `{1:eph_pk_host(32),2:nonce_host(32)}` ┬Ě 6 PAIR_REVEAL pÔćĺhost `{1:eph_pk_p(32),2:nonce_p(32)}` ┬Ě 7 PAIR_CONFIRM hostÔćĺp `{1:confirm_mac(16)}` ┬Ě 8 PAIR_DONE pÔćĺhost `{1:done_mac(16)}` ┬Ě 14 PAIR_ACK hostÔćĺp `{1:ack_mac(16)}` ┬Ě 9 RECONNECT_CHALLENGE hostÔćĺp `{1:nonce_rc(16)}` ┬Ě 10 RECONNECT_RESPONSE pÔćĺhost `{1:tag(16)}` ┬Ě 11 PAIR_ABORT either `{1:reason tstr}`. (msg_type 12=observation, 15=retired.) **PERIPHERAL SM:** recv HELLO(4)ÔćĺRETAIN persisted key, gen fresh eph+nonce, send COMMIT(5); recv HOST_REVEAL(13); send REVEAL(6); Z=X25519, reject all-zeroÔćĺABORT{bad_key}; recv CONFIRM(7) verify confirm-host MAC; send DONE(8); recv ACK(14) verify ack-host MACÔćĺ**PERSIST K**. Reconnect: recv CHALLENGE(9)Ôćĺtag=HMAC(link_key,"r2-usb-reconnect-v1"ÔÇľnonce_rcÔÇľusb_link_id)[..16]ÔćĺRESPONSE(10); activation host-local (peripheral proves to host only). Idempotent in-session dup (RAM, 60s terminal timeout): dup CONFIRMÔćĺresend DONE, dup ACKÔćĺno-op. Key preservation: persisted key retained until final ACK-verify; re-pair on any doubt (no journal/gen/rotation/crash-recovery). transcript = eph_pk_hostÔÇľeph_pk_pÔÇľnonce_hostÔÇľnonce_p (128B). usb_link_id = CAPS hive_id_bytes (16B) = HKDF("r2-usb-link-v1",device_master_secret,"")[..16].

## ­čĄŁ tn_base recipe modeling ÔÇö SPECS RULED (┬ž3.3.1 v0.30 @8c8310d); SHA-fidelity = remaining open item for core

## ­čžę WASM HOST ÔÇö LINKABLE BASE (NEW workstream, Roy GO 2026-07-10, task #64; parallel to RAK)
Roy ruled BUILD the linkable base; hive owns the **wasm HOST** (base HOSTS wasm ensemble modules = Level 2, greenfield ÔÇö NOT r2-hive-wasm, which is R2 compiled TO wasm). Ref: r2-specifications docs/proposals/R2-LINKABLE-BASE-AND-VARIANT-MANAGEMENT-2026-07-10.md (D.3 steps 4-5). **Prep design committed: docs/WASM-HOST-LINKABLE-BASE-PREP.md (c709e23).**
- **Two ABI surfaces** (both = the ┬ž12.4 Plugin trait lowered to repr(C) per proposal A.5.3): module-EXPORTS (execute/init/poll Ôćĺ wasm ptr+len) + host-IMPORTS (the capabilities.requires ┬ž12.3 syscall surface = "the host-import surface"). A wasm module becomes a Rust Plugin impl trampolining into its exports Ôćĺ plugs into existing engine dispatch.
- **Phasing (D.3 4-5, core A.5 binding):** std host (wasmtime) + browser (native WebAssembly) FIRST; then esp32s3+PSRAM wasm3; **nrf52840 = ONE bounded (<=32KB) boot-reserved wasm3 slot only** (A.5.1 ÔÇö general multi-module REFUTED; binding constraint = 64KB-page CONTIGUITY on MMU-less heap, not total RAM). **Level-0 hot-path/crypto NEVER modularized** (A.5.4 ÔÇö route/dedup/wire/CBOR/FNV, radio io_task, HMAC/HKDF/Ed25519). Host = orchestration-class only.
